\DoxyCodeLine{02194\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02195\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ To\ support\ platform\ where\ unsigned\ long\ cannot\ be\ used\ interchangeably\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02196\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ inptr\_t\ (e.g.\ CHERI-\/extended\ ISAs),\ we\ can\ use\ the\ stdint.h\ intptr\_t.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02197\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Ideally,\ we\ could\ just\ use\ (u)intptr\_t\ everywhere,\ but\ this\ could\ result\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02198\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ ABI\ breakage\ if\ khronos\_uintptr\_t\ is\ changed\ from\ unsigned\ long\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02199\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ unsigned\ long\ long\ or\ similar\ (this\ results\ in\ different\ C++\ name\ mangling).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02200\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ To\ avoid\ changes\ for\ existing\ platforms,\ we\ restrict\ usage\ of\ intptr\_t\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02201\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ platforms\ where\ the\ size\ of\ a\ pointer\ is\ larger\ than\ the\ size\ of\ long.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02202\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
